<userid>110393843681381589488</userid><username>Shawanda Buckner<//username><Date>1609492741376< /Date><rating>4</rating>< Text>
We came here on a Saturday evening around 8pm without any reservations and we were lucky to find a table.  We asked our waiter and he suggested their daily special which was the lamb shank, he also suggested their Chicken tika Masala.  He was definitely on spot with his suggestions, specifically on the lamb shank.  The lamb shank was honestly beyond what I expected.  It was very tender and juicy and the stew that covered it was full of flavor and spicy.  I order some chapati to scoop the meat and sauce and they were good also.  Before I forget also their Cheese Naan was outstanding too, the cheese was melted on the bread.  I would come again soon to try new dishes and order their cheese Naan< /Text>

They have always been helpful, and even though they forgot to pick our cans up once, they made every effort to have someone come get them ASAP (in our area, trash is only out here Thursday, so it wasn't guaranteed as they pick up other homes during the week and may not have time),  and the next day they came and got the trash. The espresso made me feel like I was back in Italy it was that great short strong not watery at all golden creamy texture. The right way. For real. I'm Sicilian I should know. It was just the way it's supposed to be. We went for our wedding anniversary and it was such a great experience the workers were so kind it was very clean and beautiful inside the prices are great also, and we were able to sit outside at their cute tables which was so nice and romantic and made for the perfect mini date! Please go to this amazing European Cafe their pastries are exquisite just as well as their cakes but I highly recommend trying the princess cake, was amazing!< /Text>

1549921358985<//date>
<Rate>2<//Rate>< text>
I have been a patron of Emil's Swiss Pastry for nearly 40 years, going back to the days when Emil Kofmel, the original owner operated this bakery. Ever since "Old Emil" handed in his towel, there has been a gradual, but steady decline. The number of different types of bakery and pastry goods offered have dwindled, also in recent times the portions have become roughly half the size than what it used to be, but the prices have increased considerably. The staff at Emil's Swiss Pastry is often sultry, if not rude. Be it what it may, it is not the customer's fault if they get poorly paid.
Also I found recently, that on the shelves occasionally day-old pastry is being offered for sale - one can easily see it on the example of the Napoleons, the custard on the edges is dried and cracked. It is too bad, for Emil's Swiss Pastry once enjoyed a stellar reputation.</text>

<user>112828439356846150614</user><user_name>Olivia Han<//user_name><Date>1620537879574< /Date><rate>5< /rate><review>Incredible experience at BHLDN thanks to the personal stylist Cezanne, and in an hour, walked out with exactly what I was looking for.

I had 2 dress appointments in one day, across different shops. The big box store I went to before BHLDN felt like a terrifying BRIDE FACTORY. Incredibly impersonal, you check in and you're left alone to browse/pick dresses for 15-20 minutes. When you're looking at 100 dresses on the rack for the first time, it's incredibly overwhelming. Was later ushered into a dressing room, and the person helping me was attending to two people - myself and another girl next to me. She couldn't keep up with both of us trying our dresses, and my mom had to step in and help clip me. Quite frankly, it wasn't a fun or enjoyable experience.

BHLDN was a whole different ballgame. After I checked in, I expected something similar to store #1: they'd pull the dresses and usher me into a dressing room for me to figure it out. Cezanne instead went through everything I'd submitted online, checked my budget, explained how alterations can quickly add up, asked if my budget was including/excluding alterations, and cross-referenced the prices of each dress I had picked out! She directed me to walk around the showroom (which was beautifully done and not overwhelming), and asked me to talk through what I liked and didn't like while asking questions to understand my tastes.

I told her my primary goal was to have a more casual dress that I could rewear every year, and she held onto EVERYTHING I said to help guide my decision. She gave such fabulous, wise advice that I wouldn't have otherwise thought of as a first-time buyer around fit, flow, etc. She was extremely perceptive to whether I loved or loathed something about a dress, and cheered me on when something wasn't my usual style, but looked good on me! Talking to her was like talking to a long-time friend who also was a wedding dress EXPERT.

Everything felt incredibly personalized, luxurious, and with her guidance I walked out of that store with the perfect dress - the Cali in ivory at $184 after tax. <Date>1617859579408< /Date><Review>Taco Bell next door? Hard pass. Looking for a better taste? El Faro. Grab a large Jamaica or a delicious Horchata with your dependable quesadillas. Feeling adventurous with the new trends? Go there on the weekend only for some birria tacos that are possibly their most delicious items. Feeling like a philly cheese steak that's improved or a memory of a state fair cheese steak sandwich? Grab the steak and cheese torta and don't look back!

From nachos to dinner plates and even a shrimp burrito, you can't go too wrong here. I'm not necessarily a fan of the steamed tortilla but they're happy to grill upon request. Nor am I'm usually thrilled about their guac because it's a little thin for my taste. But I GUARANTEE once you taste their salsa you'll be hooked. You'll never look back next door for any fire or diablo sauce. Come grab an extra salsa that's laced with a hint of habanero and thank me later.

Enjoy a meal made with consistency and don't be afraid to say hi inside.< /Review></record></dataset><record>
